2491
2492#if _USE_FIND1 && _FS_MINIMIZE0 <= 1
2493/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
2494/* Pattern matching */
2495/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
2496
2497static
2498WCHAR get_achar ( /* Get a character and advances ptr 1 or 2 */
2499 const TCHAR** ptr /* Pointer to pointer to the SBCS/DBCS/Unicode string */
2500)
2501{
2502#if !_LFN_UNICODE0
2503 WCHAR chr;
2504
2505 chr = (BYTE)*(*ptr)++; /* Get a byte */
2506 if (IsLower(chr)(((chr)>='a')&&((chr)<='z'))) chr -= 0x20; /* To upper ASCII char */
2507#ifdef _EXCVT{0x80,0x9A,0x45,0x41,0x8E,0x41,0x8F,0x80,0x45,0x45,0x45,0x49,
0x49,0x49,0x8E,0x8F, 0x90,0x92,0x92,0x4F,0x99,0x4F,0x55,0x55,
0x59,0x99,0x9A,0x9B,0x9C,0x9D,0x9E,0x9F, 0x41,0x49,0x4F,0x55,
0xA5,0xA5,0xA6,0xA7,0xA8,0xA9,0xAA,0xAB,0xAC,0xAD,0xAE,0xAF, 0xB0
,0xB1,0xB2,0xB3,0xB4,0xB5,0xB6,0xB7,0xB8,0xB9,0xBA,0xBB,0xBC,
0xBD,0xBE,0xBF, 0xC0,0xC1,0xC2,0xC3,0xC4,0xC5,0xC6,0xC7,0xC8,
0xC9,0xCA,0xCB,0xCC,0xCD,0xCE,0xCF, 0xD0,0xD1,0xD2,0xD3,0xD4,
0xD5,0xD6,0xD7,0xD8,0xD9,0xDA,0xDB,0xDC,0xDD,0xDE,0xDF, 0xE0,
0xE1,0xE2,0xE3,0xE4,0xE5,0xE6,0xE7,0xE8,0xE9,0xEA,0xEB,0xEC,0xED
,0xEE,0xEF, 0xF0,0xF1,0xF2,0xF3,0xF4,0xF5,0xF6,0xF7,0xF8,0xF9
,0xFA,0xFB,0xFC,0xFD,0xFE,0xFF}
2508 if (chr >= 0x80) chr = ExCvt[chr - 0x80]; /* To upper SBCS extended char */
2509#else
2510 if (IsDBCS1(chr)0 && IsDBCS2(**ptr)0) { /* Get DBC 2nd byte if needed */
2511 chr = chr << 8 | (BYTE)*(*ptr)++;
2512 }
2513#endif
2514 return chr;
2515#else
2516 return ff_wtoupper(*(*ptr)++); /* Get a word and to upper */
2517#endif
2518}
2519
2520
2521static
2522int pattern_matching ( /* 0:not matched, 1:matched */
2523 const TCHAR* pat, /* Matching pattern */
2524 const TCHAR* nam, /* String to be tested */
2525 int skip, /* Number of pre-skip chars (number of ?s) */
2526 int inf /* Infinite search (* specified) */
2527)
2528{
2529 const TCHAR *pp, *np;
2530 WCHAR pc, nc;
2531 int nm, nx;
2532
2533
2534 while (skip--) { /* Pre-skip name chars */
2535 if (!get_achar(&nam)) return 0; /* Branch mismatched if less name chars */
2536 }
2537 if (!*pat && inf) return 1; /* (short circuit) */
2538
2539 do {
2540 pp = pat; np = nam; /* Top of pattern and name to match */
2541 for (;;) {
2542 if (*pp == '?' || *pp == '*') { /* Wildcard? */
2543 nm = nx = 0;
2544 do { /* Analyze the wildcard chars */
2545 if (*pp++ == '?') nm++; else nx = 1;
2546 } while (*pp == '?' || *pp == '*');
2547 if (pattern_matching(pp, np, nm, nx)) return 1; /* Test new branch (recurs upto number of wildcard blocks in the pattern) */
2548 nc = *np; break; /* Branch mismatched */
2549 }
2550 pc = get_achar(&pp); /* Get a pattern char */
2551 nc = get_achar(&np); /* Get a name char */
2552 if (pc != nc) break; /* Branch mismatched? */
2553 if (pc == 0) return 1; /* Branch matched? (matched at end of both strings) */
2554 }
2555 get_achar(&nam); /* nam++ */
2556 } while (inf && nc); /* Retry until end of name if infinite search is specified */
2557
2558 return 0;
2559}
2560
2561#endif /* _USE_FIND && _FS_MINIMIZE <= 1 */
2562
2563
2564
2565/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
2566/* Pick a top segment and create the object name in directory form */
2567/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
2568
2569static
2570FRESULT create_name ( /* FR_OK: successful, FR_INVALID_NAME: could not create */
2571 DIR* dp, /* Pointer to the directory object */
2572 const TCHAR** path /* Pointer to pointer to the segment in the path string */
2573)
2574{
2575#if _USE_LFN3 != 0 /* LFN configuration */
2576 BYTE b, cf;
2577 WCHAR w, *lfn;
2578 UINT i, ni, si, di;
2579 const TCHAR *p;
2580
2581 /* Create LFN in Unicode */
2582 p = *path; lfn = dp->obj.fs->lfnbuf; si = di = 0;
2583 for (;;) {
2584 w = p[si++]; /* Get a character */
2585 if (w < ' ') break; /* Break if end of the path name */
2586 if (w == '/' || w == '\\') { /* Break if a separator is found */
2587 while (p[si] == '/' || p[si] == '\\') si++; /* Skip duplicated separator if exist */
2588 break;
2589 }
2590 if (di >= _MAX_LFN255) return FR_INVALID_NAME; /* Reject too long name */
2591#if !_LFN_UNICODE0
2592 w &= 0xFF;
2593 if (IsDBCS1(w)0) { /* Check if it is a DBC 1st byte (always false on SBCS cfg) */
2594 b = (BYTE)p[si++]; /* Get 2nd byte */
2595 w = (w << 8) + b; /* Create a DBC */
2596 if (!IsDBCS2(b)0) return FR_INVALID_NAME; /* Reject invalid sequence */
2597 }
2598 w = ff_convert(w, 1); /* Convert ANSI/OEM to Unicode */
2599 if (!w) return FR_INVALID_NAME; /* Reject invalid code */
2600#endif
2601 if (w < 0x80 && chk_chr("\"*:<>\?|\x7F", w)) return FR_INVALID_NAME; /* Reject illegal characters for LFN */
2602 lfn[di++] = w; /* Store the Unicode character */
2603 }
2604 *path = &p[si]; /* Return pointer to the next segment */
2605 cf = (w < ' ') ? NS_LAST0x04 : 0; /* Set last segment flag if end of the path */
2606#if _FS_RPATH2 != 0
2607 if ((di == 1 && lfn[di - 1] == '.') ||
2608 (di == 2 && lfn[di - 1] == '.' && lfn[di - 2] == '.')) { /* Is this segment a dot name? */
2609 lfn[di] = 0;
2610 for (i = 0; i < 11; i++) /* Create dot name for SFN entry */
2611 dp->fn[i] = (i < di) ? '.' : ' ';
2612 dp->fn[i] = cf | NS_DOT0x20; /* This is a dot entry */
2613 return FR_OK;
2614 }
2615#endif
2616 while (di) { /* Snip off trailing spaces and dots if exist */
2617 w = lfn[di - 1];
2618 if (w != ' ' && w != '.') break;
2619 di--;
2620 }
2621 lfn[di] = 0; /* LFN is created */
2622 if (di == 0) return FR_INVALID_NAME; /* Reject nul name */
2623
2624 /* Create SFN in directory form */
2625 mem_set(dp->fn, ' ', 11);
2626 for (si = 0; lfn[si] == ' ' || lfn[si] == '.'; si++) ; /* Strip leading spaces and dots */
2627 if (si) cf |= NS_LOSS0x01 | NS_LFN0x02;
2628 while (di && lfn[di - 1] != '.') di--; /* Find extension (di<=si: no extension) */
2629
2630 i = b = 0; ni = 8;
2631 for (;;) {
2632 w = lfn[si++]; /* Get an LFN character */
2633 if (!w) break; /* Break on end of the LFN */
2634 if (w == ' ' || (w == '.' && si != di)) { /* Remove spaces and dots */
2635 cf |= NS_LOSS0x01 | NS_LFN0x02; continue;
2636 }
2637
2638 if (i >= ni || si == di) { /* Extension or end of SFN */
2639 if (ni == 11) { /* Long extension */
2640 cf |= NS_LOSS0x01 | NS_LFN0x02; break;
2641 }
2642 if (si != di) cf |= NS_LOSS0x01 | NS_LFN0x02; /* Out of 8.3 format */
2643 if (si > di) break; /* No extension */
2644 si = di; i = 8; ni = 11; /* Enter extension section */
2645 b <<= 2; continue;
2646 }
2647
2648 if (w >= 0x80) { /* Non ASCII character */
2649#ifdef _EXCVT{0x80,0x9A,0x45,0x41,0x8E,0x41,0x8F,0x80,0x45,0x45,0x45,0x49,
0x49,0x49,0x8E,0x8F, 0x90,0x92,0x92,0x4F,0x99,0x4F,0x55,0x55,
0x59,0x99,0x9A,0x9B,0x9C,0x9D,0x9E,0x9F, 0x41,0x49,0x4F,0x55,
0xA5,0xA5,0xA6,0xA7,0xA8,0xA9,0xAA,0xAB,0xAC,0xAD,0xAE,0xAF, 0xB0
,0xB1,0xB2,0xB3,0xB4,0xB5,0xB6,0xB7,0xB8,0xB9,0xBA,0xBB,0xBC,
0xBD,0xBE,0xBF, 0xC0,0xC1,0xC2,0xC3,0xC4,0xC5,0xC6,0xC7,0xC8,
0xC9,0xCA,0xCB,0xCC,0xCD,0xCE,0xCF, 0xD0,0xD1,0xD2,0xD3,0xD4,
0xD5,0xD6,0xD7,0xD8,0xD9,0xDA,0xDB,0xDC,0xDD,0xDE,0xDF, 0xE0,
0xE1,0xE2,0xE3,0xE4,0xE5,0xE6,0xE7,0xE8,0xE9,0xEA,0xEB,0xEC,0xED
,0xEE,0xEF, 0xF0,0xF1,0xF2,0xF3,0xF4,0xF5,0xF6,0xF7,0xF8,0xF9
,0xFA,0xFB,0xFC,0xFD,0xFE,0xFF}
2650 w = ff_convert(w, 0); /* Unicode -> OEM code */
2651 if (w) w = ExCvt[w - 0x80]; /* Convert extended character to upper (SBCS) */
2652#else
2653 w = ff_convert(ff_wtoupper(w), 0); /* Upper converted Unicode -> OEM code */
2654#endif
2655 cf |= NS_LFN0x02; /* Force create LFN entry */
2656 }
2657
2658 if (_DF1S0 && w >= 0x100) { /* Is this DBC? (always false at SBCS cfg) */
2659 if (i >= ni - 1) {
2660 cf |= NS_LOSS0x01 | NS_LFN0x02; i = ni; continue;
2661 }
2662 dp->fn[i++] = (BYTE)(w >> 8);
2663 } else { /* SBC */
2664 if (!w || chk_chr("+,;=[]", w)) { /* Replace illegal characters for SFN */
2665 w = '_'; cf |= NS_LOSS0x01 | NS_LFN0x02;/* Lossy conversion */
2666 } else {
2667 if (IsUpper(w)(((w)>='A')&&((w)<='Z'))) { /* ASCII large capital */
2668 b |= 2;
2669 } else {
2670 if (IsLower(w)(((w)>='a')&&((w)<='z'))) { /* ASCII small capital */
2671 b |= 1; w -= 0x20;
2672 }
2673 }
2674 }
2675 }
2676 dp->fn[i++] = (BYTE)w;
2677 }
2678
2679 if (dp->fn[0] == DDEM0xE5) dp->fn[0] = RDDEM0x05; /* If the first character collides with DDEM, replace it with RDDEM */
2680
2681 if (ni == 8) b <<= 2;
2682 if ((b & 0x0C) == 0x0C || (b & 0x03) == 0x03) cf |= NS_LFN0x02; /* Create LFN entry when there are composite capitals */
2683 if (!(cf & NS_LFN0x02)) { /* When LFN is in 8.3 format without extended character, NT flags are created */
2684 if ((b & 0x03) == 0x01) cf |= NS_EXT0x10; /* NT flag (Extension has only small capital) */
2685 if ((b & 0x0C) == 0x04) cf |= NS_BODY0x08; /* NT flag (Filename has only small capital) */
2686 }
2687
2688 dp->fn[NSFLAG11] = cf; /* SFN is created */
2689
2690 return FR_OK;
2691
2692
2693#else /* _USE_LFN != 0 : Non-LFN configuration */
2694 BYTE c, d, *sfn;
2695 UINT ni, si, i;
2696 const char *p;
2697
2698 /* Create file name in directory form */
2699 p = *path; sfn = dp->fn;
2700 mem_set(sfn, ' ', 11);
2701 si = i = 0; ni = 8;
2702#if _FS_RPATH2 != 0
2703 if (p[si] == '.') { /* Is this a dot entry? */
2704 for (;;) {
2705 c = (BYTE)p[si++];
2706 if (c != '.' || si >= 3) break;
2707 sfn[i++] = c;
2708 }
2709 if (c != '/' && c != '\\' && c > ' ') return FR_INVALID_NAME;
2710 *path = p + si; /* Return pointer to the next segment */
2711 sfn[NSFLAG11] = (c <= ' ') ? NS_LAST0x04 | NS_DOT0x20 : NS_DOT0x20; /* Set last segment flag if end of the path */
2712 return FR_OK;
2713 }
2714#endif
2715 for (;;) {
2716 c = (BYTE)p[si++];
2717 if (c <= ' ') break; /* Break if end of the path name */
2718 if (c == '/' || c == '\\') { /* Break if a separator is found */
2719 while (p[si] == '/' || p[si] == '\\') si++; /* Skip duplicated separator if exist */
2720 break;
2721 }
2722 if (c == '.' || i >= ni) { /* End of body or over size? */
2723 if (ni == 11 || c != '.') return FR_INVALID_NAME; /* Over size or invalid dot */
2724 i = 8; ni = 11; /* Goto extension */
2725 continue;
2726 }
2727 if (c >= 0x80) { /* Extended character? */
2728#ifdef _EXCVT{0x80,0x9A,0x45,0x41,0x8E,0x41,0x8F,0x80,0x45,0x45,0x45,0x49,
0x49,0x49,0x8E,0x8F, 0x90,0x92,0x92,0x4F,0x99,0x4F,0x55,0x55,
0x59,0x99,0x9A,0x9B,0x9C,0x9D,0x9E,0x9F, 0x41,0x49,0x4F,0x55,
0xA5,0xA5,0xA6,0xA7,0xA8,0xA9,0xAA,0xAB,0xAC,0xAD,0xAE,0xAF, 0xB0
,0xB1,0xB2,0xB3,0xB4,0xB5,0xB6,0xB7,0xB8,0xB9,0xBA,0xBB,0xBC,
0xBD,0xBE,0xBF, 0xC0,0xC1,0xC2,0xC3,0xC4,0xC5,0xC6,0xC7,0xC8,
0xC9,0xCA,0xCB,0xCC,0xCD,0xCE,0xCF, 0xD0,0xD1,0xD2,0xD3,0xD4,
0xD5,0xD6,0xD7,0xD8,0xD9,0xDA,0xDB,0xDC,0xDD,0xDE,0xDF, 0xE0,
0xE1,0xE2,0xE3,0xE4,0xE5,0xE6,0xE7,0xE8,0xE9,0xEA,0xEB,0xEC,0xED
,0xEE,0xEF, 0xF0,0xF1,0xF2,0xF3,0xF4,0xF5,0xF6,0xF7,0xF8,0xF9
,0xFA,0xFB,0xFC,0xFD,0xFE,0xFF}
2729 c = ExCvt[c - 0x80]; /* To upper extended characters (SBCS cfg) */
2730#else
2731#if !_DF1S0
2732 return FR_INVALID_NAME; /* Reject extended characters (ASCII only cfg) */
2733#endif
2734#endif
2735 }
2736 if (IsDBCS1(c)0) { /* Check if it is a DBC 1st byte (always false at SBCS cfg.) */
2737 d = (BYTE)p[si++]; /* Get 2nd byte */
2738 if (!IsDBCS2(d)0 || i >= ni - 1) return FR_INVALID_NAME; /* Reject invalid DBC */
2739 sfn[i++] = c;
2740 sfn[i++] = d;
2741 } else { /* SBC */
2742 if (chk_chr("\"*+,:;<=>\?[]|\x7F", c)) return FR_INVALID_NAME; /* Reject illegal chrs for SFN */
2743 if (IsLower(c)(((c)>='a')&&((c)<='z'))) c -= 0x20; /* To upper */
2744 sfn[i++] = c;
2745 }
2746 }
2747 *path = p + si; /* Return pointer to the next segment */
2748 if (i == 0) return FR_INVALID_NAME; /* Reject nul string */
2749
2750 if (sfn[0] == DDEM0xE5) sfn[0] = RDDEM0x05; /* If the first character collides with DDEM, replace it with RDDEM */
2751 sfn[NSFLAG11] = (c <= ' ') ? NS_LAST0x04 : 0; /* Set last segment flag if end of the path */
2752
2753 return FR_OK;
2754#endif /* _USE_LFN != 0 */
2755}
2756
2757
2758
2759
2760/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
2761/* Follow a file path */
2762/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
2763
2764static
2765FRESULT follow_path ( /* FR_OK(0): successful, !=0: error code */
2766 DIR* dp, /* Directory object to return last directory and found object */
2767 const TCHAR* path /* Full-path string to find a file or directory */
2768)
2769{
2770 FRESULT res;
2771 BYTE ns;
2772 _FDID *obj = &dp->obj;
2773 FATFS *fs = obj->fs;
2774
2775
2776#if _FS_RPATH2 != 0
2777 if (*path != '/' && *path != '\\') { /* Without heading separator */
2778 obj->sclust = fs->cdir; /* Start from the current directory */
2779 } else
2780#endif
2781 { /* With heading separator */
2782 while (*path == '/' || *path == '\\') path++; /* Strip heading separator */
2783 obj->sclust = 0; /* Start from the root directory */
2784 }
2785#if _FS_EXFAT1 && _FS_RPATH2 != 0
2786 if (fs->fs_type == FS_EXFAT4 && obj->sclust) { /* Retrieve the sub-directory status if needed */
2787 DIR dj;
2788
2789 obj->c_scl = fs->cdc_scl;
2790 obj->c_size = fs->cdc_size;
2791 obj->c_ofs = fs->cdc_ofs;
2792 res = load_obj_dir(&dj, obj);
2793 if (res != FR_OK) return res;
2794 obj->objsize = ld_dword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FileSize56);
2795 obj->stat = fs->dirbuf[XDIR_GenFlags33] & 2;
2796 }
2797#endif
2798
2799 if ((UINT)*path < ' ') { /* Null path name is the origin directory itself */
2800 dp->fn[NSFLAG11] = NS_NONAME0x80;
2801 res = dir_sdi(dp, 0);
2802
2803 } else { /* Follow path */
2804 for (;;) {
2805 res = create_name(dp, &path); /* Get a segment name of the path */
2806 if (res != FR_OK) break;
2807 res = dir_find(dp); /* Find an object with the segment name */
2808 ns = dp->fn[NSFLAG11];
2809 if (res != FR_OK) { /* Failed to find the object */
2810 if (res == FR_NO_FILE) { /* Object is not found */
2811 if (_FS_RPATH2 && (ns & NS_DOT0x20)) { /* If dot entry is not exist, stay there */
2812 if (!(ns & NS_LAST0x04)) continue; /* Continue to follow if not last segment */
2813 dp->fn[NSFLAG11] = NS_NONAME0x80;
2814 res = FR_OK;
2815 } else { /* Could not find the object */
2816 if (!(ns & NS_LAST0x04)) res = FR_NO_PATH; /* Adjust error code if not last segment */
2817 }
2818 }
2819 break;
2820 }
2821 if (ns & NS_LAST0x04) break; /* Last segment matched. Function completed. */
2822 /* Get into the sub-directory */
2823 if (!(obj->attr & AM_DIR0x10)) { /* It is not a sub-directory and cannot follow */
2824 res = FR_NO_PATH; break;
2825 }
2826#if _FS_EXFAT1
2827 if (fs->fs_type == FS_EXFAT4) {
2828 obj->c_scl = obj->sclust; /* Save containing directory information for next dir */
2829 obj->c_size = ((DWORD)obj->objsize & 0xFFFFFF00) | obj->stat;
2830 obj->c_ofs = dp->blk_ofs;
2831 obj->sclust = ld_dword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FstClus52); /* Open next directory */
2832 obj->stat = fs->dirbuf[XDIR_GenFlags33] & 2;
2833 obj->objsize = ld_qword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FileSize56);
2834 } else
2835#endif
2836 {
2837 obj->sclust = ld_clust(fs, fs->win + dp->dptr % SS(fs)((UINT)512)); /* Open next directory */
2838 }
2839 }
2840 }
2841
2842 return res;
2843}
2844
2845
2846
2847
2848/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
2849/* Get logical drive number from path name */
2850/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
2851
2852static
2853int get_ldnumber ( /* Returns logical drive number (-1:invalid drive) */
2854 const TCHAR** path /* Pointer to pointer to the path name */
2855)
2856{
2857 const TCHAR *tp, *tt;
2858 UINT i;
2859 int vol = -1;
2860#if _STR_VOLUME_ID0 /* Find string drive id */
2861 static const char* const str[] = {_VOLUME_STRS"RAM","NAND","CF","SD","SD2","USB","USB2","USB3"};
2862 const char *sp;
2863 char c;
2864 TCHAR tc;
2865#endif
2866
2867
2868 if (*path) { /* If the pointer is not a null */
2869 for (tt = *path; (UINT)*tt >= (_USE_LFN3 ? ' ' : '!') && *tt != ':'; tt++) ; /* Find ':' in the path */
2870 if (*tt == ':') { /* If a ':' is exist in the path name */
2871 tp = *path;
2872 i = *tp++ - '0';
2873 if (i < 10 && tp == tt) { /* Is there a numeric drive id? */
2874 if (i < _VOLUMES1) { /* If a drive id is found, get the value and strip it */
2875 vol = (int)i;
2876 *path = ++tt;
2877 }
2878 }
2879#if _STR_VOLUME_ID0
2880 else { /* No numeric drive number, find string drive id */
2881 i = 0; tt++;
2882 do {
2883 sp = str[i]; tp = *path;
2884 do { /* Compare a string drive id with path name */
2885 c = *sp++; tc = *tp++;
2886 if (IsLower(tc)(((tc)>='a')&&((tc)<='z'))) tc -= 0x20;
2887 } while (c && (TCHAR)c == tc);
2888 } while ((c || tp != tt) && ++i < _VOLUMES1); /* Repeat for each id until pattern match */
2889 if (i < _VOLUMES1) { /* If a drive id is found, get the value and strip it */
2890 vol = (int)i;
2891 *path = tt;
2892 }
2893 }
2894#endif
2895 return vol;
2896 }
2897#if _FS_RPATH2 != 0 && _VOLUMES1 >= 2
2898 vol = CurrVol; /* Current drive */
2899#else
2900 vol = 0; /* Drive 0 */
2901#endif
2902 }
2903 return vol;
2904}
2905
2906
2907
2908
2909/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
2910/* Load a sector and check if it is an FAT boot sector */
2911/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
2912
2913static
2914BYTE check_fs ( /* 0:FAT, 1:exFAT, 2:Valid BS but not FAT, 3:Not a BS, 4:Disk error */
2915 FATFS* fs, /* File system object */
2916 DWORD sect /* Sector# (lba) to check if it is an FAT-VBR or not */
2917)
2918{
2919 fs->wflag = 0; fs->winsect = 0xFFFFFFFF; /* Invaidate window */
2920 if (move_window(fs, sect) != FR_OK) return 4; /* Load boot record */
2921
2922 if (ld_word(fs->win + BS_55AA510) != 0xAA55) return 3; /* Check boot record signature (always placed at offset 510 even if the sector size is >512) */
2923
2924 if (fs->win[BS_JmpBoot0] == 0xE9 || (fs->win[BS_JmpBoot0] == 0xEB && fs->win[BS_JmpBoot0 + 2] == 0x90)) {
2925 if ((ld_dword(fs->win + BS_FilSysType54) & 0xFFFFFF) == 0x544146) return 0; /* Check "FAT" string */
2926 if (ld_dword(fs->win + BS_FilSysType3282) == 0x33544146) return 0; /* Check "FAT3" string */
2927 }
2928#if _FS_EXFAT1
2929 if (!mem_cmp(fs->win + BS_JmpBoot0, "\xEB\x76\x90" "EXFAT ", 11)) return 1;
2930#endif
2931 return 2;
2932}
2933
2934
2935
2936
2937/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
2938/* Find logical drive and check if the volume is mounted */
2939/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
2940
2941static
2942FRESULT find_volume ( /* FR_OK(0): successful, !=0: any error occurred */
2943 const TCHAR** path, /* Pointer to pointer to the path name (drive number) */
2944 FATFS** rfs, /* Pointer to pointer to the found file system object */
2945 BYTE mode /* !=0: Check write protection for write access */
2946)
2947{
2948 BYTE fmt, *pt;
2949 int vol;
2950 DSTATUS stat;
2951 DWORD bsect, fasize, tsect, sysect, nclst, szbfat, br[4];
2952 WORD nrsv;
2953 FATFS *fs;
2954 UINT i;
2955
2956
2957 /* Get logical drive number */
2958 *rfs = 0;
2959 vol = get_ldnumber(path);
2960 if (vol < 0) return FR_INVALID_DRIVE;
2961
2962 /* Check if the file system object is valid or not */
2963 fs = FatFs[vol]; /* Get pointer to the file system object */
2964 if (!fs) return FR_NOT_ENABLED; /* Is the file system object available? */
2965
2966 ENTER_FF(fs); /* Lock the volume */
2967 *rfs = fs; /* Return pointer to the file system object */
2968
2969 mode &= (BYTE)~FA_READ0x01; /* Desired access mode, write access or not */
2970 if (fs->fs_type) { /* If the volume has been mounted */
2971 stat = disk_status(fs->drv);
2972 if (!(stat & STA_NOINIT0x01)) { /* and the physical drive is kept initialized */
2973 if (!_FS_READONLY0 && mode && (stat & STA_PROTECT0x04)) { /* Check write protection if needed */
2974 return FR_WRITE_PROTECTED;
2975 }
2976 return FR_OK; /* The file system object is valid */
2977 }
2978 }
2979
2980 /* The file system object is not valid. */
2981 /* Following code attempts to mount the volume. (analyze BPB and initialize the fs object) */
2982
2983 fs->fs_type = 0; /* Clear the file system object */
2984 fs->drv = LD2PD(vol)(BYTE)(vol); /* Bind the logical drive and a physical drive */
2985 stat = disk_initialize(fs->drv); /* Initialize the physical drive */
2986 if (stat & STA_NOINIT0x01) { /* Check if the initialization succeeded */
2987 return FR_NOT_READY; /* Failed to initialize due to no medium or hard error */
2988 }
2989 if (!_FS_READONLY0 && mode && (stat & STA_PROTECT0x04)) { /* Check disk write protection if needed */
2990 return FR_WRITE_PROTECTED;
2991 }
2992#if _MAX_SS512 != _MIN_SS512 /* Get sector size (multiple sector size cfg only) */
2993 if (disk_ioctl(fs->drv, GET_SECTOR_SIZE2, &SS(fs)((UINT)512)) != RES_OK) return FR_DISK_ERR;
2994 if (SS(fs)((UINT)512) > _MAX_SS512 || SS(fs)((UINT)512) < _MIN_SS512 || (SS(fs)((UINT)512) & (SS(fs)((UINT)512) - 1))) return FR_DISK_ERR;
2995#endif
2996 /* Find an FAT partition on the drive. Supports only generic partitioning, FDISK and SFD. */
2997 bsect = 0;
2998 fmt = check_fs(fs, bsect); /* Load sector 0 and check if it is an FAT-VBR as SFD */
2999 if (fmt == 2 || (fmt < 2 && LD2PT(vol)0 != 0)) { /* Not an FAT-VBR or forced partition number */
3000 for (i = 0; i < 4; i++) { /* Get partition offset */
3001 pt = fs->win + (MBR_Table446 + i * SZ_PTE16);
3002 br[i] = pt[PTE_System4] ? ld_dword(pt + PTE_StLba8) : 0;
3003 }
3004 i = LD2PT(vol)0; /* Partition number: 0:auto, 1-4:forced */
3005 if (i) i--;
3006 do { /* Find an FAT volume */
3007 bsect = br[i];
3008 fmt = bsect ? check_fs(fs, bsect) : 3; /* Check the partition */
3009 } while (!LD2PT(vol)0 && fmt >= 2 && ++i < 4);
3010 }
3011 if (fmt == 4) return FR_DISK_ERR; /* An error occured in the disk I/O layer */
3012 if (fmt >= 2) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* No FAT volume is found */
3013
3014 /* An FAT volume is found. Following code initializes the file system object */
3015
3016#if _FS_EXFAT1
3017 if (fmt == 1) {
3018 QWORD maxlba;
3019
3020 for (i = BPB_ZeroedEx11; i < BPB_ZeroedEx11 + 53 && fs->win[i] == 0; i++) ; /* Check zero filler */
3021 if (i < BPB_ZeroedEx11 + 53) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM;
3022
3023 if (ld_word(fs->win + BPB_FSVerEx104) != 0x100) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* Check exFAT revision (Must be 1.0) */
3024
3025 if (1 << fs->win[BPB_BytsPerSecEx108] != SS(fs)((UINT)512)) /* (BPB_BytsPerSecEx must be equal to the physical sector size) */
3026 return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM;
3027
3028 maxlba = ld_qword(fs->win + BPB_TotSecEx72) + bsect; /* Last LBA + 1 of the volume */
3029 if (maxlba >= 0x100000000) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (It cannot be handled in 32-bit LBA) */
3030
3031 fs->fsize = ld_dword(fs->win + BPB_FatSzEx84); /* Number of sectors per FAT */
3032
3033 fs->n_fats = fs->win[BPB_NumFATsEx110]; /* Number of FATs */
3034 if (fs->n_fats != 1) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (Supports only 1 FAT) */
3035
3036 fs->csize = 1 << fs->win[BPB_SecPerClusEx109]; /* Cluster size */
3037 if (fs->csize == 0) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (Must be 1..32768) */
3038
3039 nclst = ld_dword(fs->win + BPB_NumClusEx92); /* Number of clusters */
3040 if (nclst > MAX_EXFAT0x7FFFFFFD) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (Too many clusters) */
3041 fs->n_fatent = nclst + 2;
3042
3043 /* Boundaries and Limits */
3044 fs->volbase = bsect;
3045 fs->database = bsect + ld_dword(fs->win + BPB_DataOfsEx88);
3046 fs->fatbase = bsect + ld_dword(fs->win + BPB_FatOfsEx80);
3047 if (maxlba < (QWORD)fs->database + nclst * fs->csize) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (Volume size must not be smaller than the size requiered) */
3048 fs->dirbase = ld_dword(fs->win + BPB_RootClusEx96);
3049
3050 /* Check if bitmap location is in assumption (at the first cluster) */
3051 if (move_window(fs, clust2sect(fs, fs->dirbase)) != FR_OK) return FR_DISK_ERR;
3052 for (i = 0; i < SS(fs)((UINT)512); i += SZDIRE32) {
3053 if (fs->win[i] == 0x81 && ld_dword(fs->win + i + 20) == 2) break; /* 81 entry with cluster #2? */
3054 }
3055 if (i == SS(fs)((UINT)512)) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM;
3056#if !_FS_READONLY0
3057 fs->last_clst = fs->free_clst = 0xFFFFFFFF; /* Initialize cluster allocation information */
3058#endif
3059 fmt = FS_EXFAT4; /* FAT sub-type */
3060 } else
3061#endif /* _FS_EXFAT */
3062 {
3063 if (ld_word(fs->win + BPB_BytsPerSec11) != SS(fs)((UINT)512)) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (BPB_BytsPerSec must be equal to the physical sector size) */
3064
3065 fasize = ld_word(fs->win + BPB_FATSz1622); /* Number of sectors per FAT */
3066 if (fasize == 0) fasize = ld_dword(fs->win + BPB_FATSz3236);
3067 fs->fsize = fasize;
3068
3069 fs->n_fats = fs->win[BPB_NumFATs16]; /* Number of FATs */
3070 if (fs->n_fats != 1 && fs->n_fats != 2) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (Must be 1 or 2) */
3071 fasize *= fs->n_fats; /* Number of sectors for FAT area */
3072
3073 fs->csize = fs->win[BPB_SecPerClus13]; /* Cluster size */
3074 if (fs->csize == 0 || (fs->csize & (fs->csize - 1))) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (Must be power of 2) */
3075
3076 fs->n_rootdir = ld_word(fs->win + BPB_RootEntCnt17); /* Number of root directory entries */
3077 if (fs->n_rootdir % (SS(fs)((UINT)512) / SZDIRE32)) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (Must be sector aligned) */
3078
3079 tsect = ld_word(fs->win + BPB_TotSec1619); /* Number of sectors on the volume */
3080 if (tsect == 0) tsect = ld_dword(fs->win + BPB_TotSec3232);
3081
3082 nrsv = ld_word(fs->win + BPB_RsvdSecCnt14); /* Number of reserved sectors */
3083 if (nrsv == 0) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (Must not be 0) */
3084
3085 /* Determine the FAT sub type */
3086 sysect = nrsv + fasize + fs->n_rootdir / (SS(fs)((UINT)512) / SZDIRE32); /* RSV + FAT + DIR */
3087 if (tsect < sysect) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (Invalid volume size) */
3088 nclst = (tsect - sysect) / fs->csize; /* Number of clusters */
3089 if (nclst == 0) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (Invalid volume size) */
3090 fmt = FS_FAT323;
3091 if (nclst <= MAX_FAT160xFFF5) fmt = FS_FAT162;
3092 if (nclst <= MAX_FAT120xFF5) fmt = FS_FAT121;
3093
3094 /* Boundaries and Limits */
3095 fs->n_fatent = nclst + 2; /* Number of FAT entries */
3096 fs->volbase = bsect; /* Volume start sector */
3097 fs->fatbase = bsect + nrsv; /* FAT start sector */
3098 fs->database = bsect + sysect; /* Data start sector */
3099 if (fmt == FS_FAT323) {
3100 if (ld_word(fs->win + BPB_FSVer3242) != 0) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (Must be FAT32 revision 0.0) */
3101 if (fs->n_rootdir) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (BPB_RootEntCnt must be 0) */
3102 fs->dirbase = ld_dword(fs->win + BPB_RootClus3244); /* Root directory start cluster */
3103 szbfat = fs->n_fatent * 4; /* (Needed FAT size) */
3104 } else {
3105 if (fs->n_rootdir == 0) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM;/* (BPB_RootEntCnt must not be 0) */
3106 fs->dirbase = fs->fatbase + fasize; /* Root directory start sector */
3107 szbfat = (fmt == FS_FAT162) ? /* (Needed FAT size) */
3108 fs->n_fatent * 2 : fs->n_fatent * 3 / 2 + (fs->n_fatent & 1);
3109 }
3110 if (fs->fsize < (szbfat + (SS(fs)((UINT)512) - 1)) / SS(fs)((UINT)512)) return FR_NO_FILESYSTEM; /* (BPB_FATSz must not be less than the size needed) */
3111
3112#if !_FS_READONLY0
3113 /* Get FSINFO if available */
3114 fs->last_clst = fs->free_clst = 0xFFFFFFFF; /* Initialize cluster allocation information */
3115 fs->fsi_flag = 0x80;
3116#if (_FS_NOFSINFO3 & 3) != 3
3117 if (fmt == FS_FAT323 /* Enable FSINFO only if FAT32 and BPB_FSInfo32 == 1 */
3118 && ld_word(fs->win + BPB_FSInfo3248) == 1
3119 && move_window(fs, bsect + 1) == FR_OK)
3120 {
3121 fs->fsi_flag = 0;
3122 if (ld_word(fs->win + BS_55AA510) == 0xAA55 /* Load FSINFO data if available */
3123 && ld_dword(fs->win + FSI_LeadSig0) == 0x41615252
3124 && ld_dword(fs->win + FSI_StrucSig484) == 0x61417272)
3125 {
3126#if (_FS_NOFSINFO3 & 1) == 0
3127 fs->free_clst = ld_dword(fs->win + FSI_Free_Count488);
3128#endif
3129#if (_FS_NOFSINFO3 & 2) == 0
3130 fs->last_clst = ld_dword(fs->win + FSI_Nxt_Free492);
3131#endif
3132 }
3133 }
3134#endif /* (_FS_NOFSINFO & 3) != 3 */
3135#endif /* !_FS_READONLY */
3136 }
3137
3138 fs->fs_type = fmt; /* FAT sub-type */
3139 fs->id = ++Fsid; /* File system mount ID */
3140#if _USE_LFN3 == 1
3141 fs->lfnbuf = LfnBuf; /* Static LFN working buffer */
3142#if _FS_EXFAT1
3143 fs->dirbuf = DirBuf; /* Static directory block working buuffer */
3144#endif
3145#endif
3146#if _FS_RPATH2 != 0
3147 fs->cdir = 0; /* Initialize current directory */
3148#endif
3149#if _FS_LOCK0 != 0 /* Clear file lock semaphores */
3150 clear_lock(fs);
3151#endif
3152 return FR_OK;
3153}
3154
3155
3156
3157
3158/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3159/* Check if the file/directory object is valid or not */
3160/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3161
3162static
3163FRESULT validate ( /* Returns FR_OK or FR_INVALID_OBJECT */
3164 _FDID* obj, /* Pointer to the _OBJ, the 1st member in the FIL/DIR object, to check validity */
3165 FATFS** fs /* Pointer to pointer to the owner file system object to return */
3166)
3167{
3168 FRESULT res;
3169
3170
3171 if (!obj || !obj->fs || !obj->fs->fs_type || obj->fs->id != obj->id || (disk_status(obj->fs->drv) & STA_NOINIT0x01)) {
3172 *fs = 0; /* The object is invalid */
3173 res = FR_INVALID_OBJECT;
3174 } else {
3175 *fs = obj->fs; /* Owner file sytem object */
3176 ENTER_FF(obj->fs); /* Lock file system */
3177 res = FR_OK;
3178 }
3179 return res;
3180}

3185/*---------------------------------------------------------------------------
3186
3187 Public Functions (FatFs API)
3188
3189----------------------------------------------------------------------------*/

3191
3192
3193/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3194/* Mount/Unmount a Logical Drive */
3195/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3196
3197FRESULT f_mount (
3198 FATFS* fs, /* Pointer to the file system object (NULL:unmount)*/
3199 const TCHAR* path, /* Logical drive number to be mounted/unmounted */
3200 BYTE opt /* Mode option 0:Do not mount (delayed mount), 1:Mount immediately */
3201)
3202{
3203 FATFS *cfs;
3204 int vol;
3205 FRESULT res;
3206 const TCHAR *rp = path;
3207
3208
3209 /* Get logical drive number */
3210 vol = get_ldnumber(&rp);
3211 if (vol < 0) return FR_INVALID_DRIVE;
3212 cfs = FatFs[vol]; /* Pointer to fs object */
3213
3214 if (cfs) {
3215#if _FS_LOCK0 != 0
3216 clear_lock(cfs);
3217#endif
3218#if _FS_REENTRANT0 /* Discard sync object of the current volume */
3219 if (!ff_del_syncobj(cfs->sobj)) return FR_INT_ERR;
3220#endif
3221 cfs->fs_type = 0; /* Clear old fs object */
3222 }
3223
3224 if (fs) {
3225 fs->fs_type = 0; /* Clear new fs object */
3226#if _FS_REENTRANT0 /* Create sync object for the new volume */
3227 if (!ff_cre_syncobj((BYTE)vol, &fs->sobj)) return FR_INT_ERR;
3228#endif
3229 }
3230 FatFs[vol] = fs; /* Register new fs object */
3231
3232 if (!fs || opt != 1) return FR_OK; /* Do not mount now, it will be mounted later */
3233
3234 res = find_volume(&path, &fs, 0); /* Force mounted the volume */
3235 LEAVE_FF(fs, res)return res;
3236}
3237
3238
3239
3240
3241/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3242/* Open or Create a File */
3243/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3244
3245FRESULT f_open (
3246 FIL* fp, /* Pointer to the blank file object */
3247 const TCHAR* path, /* Pointer to the file name */
3248 BYTE mode /* Access mode and file open mode flags */
3249)
3250{
3251 FRESULT res;
3252 DIR dj;
3253 FATFS *fs;
3254#if !_FS_READONLY0
3255 DWORD dw, cl, bcs, clst, sc;
3256 FSIZE_t ofs;
3257#endif
3258 DEF_NAMBUFWCHAR *lfn;
3259
3260
3261 if (!fp) return FR_INVALID_OBJECT;
3262
3263 /* Get logical drive */
3264 mode &= _FS_READONLY0 ? FA_READ0x01 : FA_READ0x01 | FA_WRITE0x02 | FA_CREATE_ALWAYS0x08 | FA_CREATE_NEW0x04 | FA_OPEN_ALWAYS0x10 | FA_OPEN_APPEND0x30 | FA_SEEKEND0x20;
3265 res = find_volume(&path, &fs, mode);
3266 if (res == FR_OK) {
3267 dj.obj.fs = fs;
3268 INIT_NAMBUF(fs){ lfn = ff_memalloc((255 +1)*2 + 32*19); if (!lfn) return FR_NOT_ENOUGH_CORE
; (fs)->lfnbuf = lfn; (fs)->dirbuf = (BYTE*)(lfn+255 +1
); };
3269 res = follow_path(&dj, path); /* Follow the file path */
3270#if !_FS_READONLY0 /* R/W configuration */
3271 if (res == FR_OK) {
3272 if (dj.fn[NSFLAG11] & NS_NONAME0x80) { /* Origin directory itself? */
3273 res = FR_INVALID_NAME;
3274 }
3275#if _FS_LOCK0 != 0
3276 else {
3277 res = chk_lock(&dj, (mode & ~FA_READ0x01) ? 1 : 0);
3278 }
3279#endif
3280 }
3281 /* Create or Open a file */
3282 if (mode & (FA_CREATE_ALWAYS0x08 | FA_OPEN_ALWAYS0x10 | FA_CREATE_NEW0x04)) {
3283 if (res != FR_OK) { /* No file, create new */
3284 if (res == FR_NO_FILE) /* There is no file to open, create a new entry */
3285#if _FS_LOCK0 != 0
3286 res = enq_lock() ? dir_register(&dj) : FR_TOO_MANY_OPEN_FILES;
3287#else
3288 res = dir_register(&dj);
3289#endif
3290 mode |= FA_CREATE_ALWAYS0x08; /* File is created */
3291 }
3292 else { /* Any object is already existing */
3293 if (dj.obj.attr & (AM_RDO0x01 | AM_DIR0x10)) { /* Cannot overwrite it (R/O or DIR) */
3294 res = FR_DENIED;
3295 } else {
3296 if (mode & FA_CREATE_NEW0x04) res = FR_EXIST; /* Cannot create as new file */
3297 }
3298 }
3299 if (res == FR_OK && (mode & FA_CREATE_ALWAYS0x08)) { /* Truncate it if overwrite mode */
3300 dw = GET_FATTIME()get_fattime();
3301#if _FS_EXFAT1
3302 if (fs->fs_type == FS_EXFAT4) {
3303 /* Get current allocation info */
3304 fp->obj.fs = fs;
3305 fp->obj.sclust = ld_dword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FstClus52);
3306 fp->obj.objsize = ld_qword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FileSize56);
3307 fp->obj.stat = fs->dirbuf[XDIR_GenFlags33] & 2;
3308 /* Initialize directory entry block */
3309 st_dword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_CrtTime8, dw); /* Set created time */
3310 fs->dirbuf[XDIR_CrtTime1020] = 0;
3311 st_dword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_ModTime12, dw); /* Set modified time */
3312 fs->dirbuf[XDIR_ModTime1021] = 0;
3313 fs->dirbuf[XDIR_Attr4] = AM_ARC0x20; /* Reset attribute */
3314 st_dword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FstClus52, 0); /* Reset file allocation info */
3315 st_qword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FileSize56, 0);
3316 st_qword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_ValidFileSize40, 0);
3317 fs->dirbuf[XDIR_GenFlags33] = 1;
3318 res = store_xdir(&dj);
3319 if (res == FR_OK && fp->obj.sclust) { /* Remove the cluster chain if exist */
3320 res = remove_chain(&fp->obj, fp->obj.sclust, 0);
3321 fs->last_clst = fp->obj.sclust - 1; /* Reuse the cluster hole */
3322 }
3323 } else
3324#endif
3325 {
3326 /* Clean directory info */
3327 st_dword(dj.dir + DIR_CrtTime14, dw); /* Set created time */
3328 st_dword(dj.dir + DIR_ModTime22, dw); /* Set modified time */
3329 dj.dir[DIR_Attr11] = AM_ARC0x20; /* Reset attribute */
3330 cl = ld_clust(fs, dj.dir); /* Get cluster chain */
3331 st_clust(fs, dj.dir, 0); /* Reset file allocation info */
3332 st_dword(dj.dir + DIR_FileSize28, 0);
3333 fs->wflag = 1;
3334
3335 if (cl) { /* Remove the cluster chain if exist */
3336 dw = fs->winsect;
3337 res = remove_chain(&dj.obj, cl, 0);
3338 if (res == FR_OK) {
3339 res = move_window(fs, dw);
3340 fs->last_clst = cl - 1; /* Reuse the cluster hole */
3341 }
3342 }
3343 }
3344 }
3345 }
3346 else { /* Open an existing file */
3347 if (res == FR_OK) { /* Following succeeded */
3348 if (dj.obj.attr & AM_DIR0x10) { /* It is a directory */
3349 res = FR_NO_FILE;
3350 } else {
3351 if ((mode & FA_WRITE0x02) && (dj.obj.attr & AM_RDO0x01)) { /* R/O violation */
3352 res = FR_DENIED;
3353 }
3354 }
3355 }
3356 }
3357 if (res == FR_OK) {
3358 if (mode & FA_CREATE_ALWAYS0x08) /* Set file change flag if created or overwritten */
3359 mode |= FA_MODIFIED0x40;
3360 fp->dir_sect = fs->winsect; /* Pointer to the directory entry */
3361 fp->dir_ptr = dj.dir;
3362#if _FS_LOCK0 != 0
3363 fp->obj.lockid = inc_lock(&dj, (mode & ~FA_READ0x01) ? 1 : 0);
3364 if (!fp->obj.lockid) res = FR_INT_ERR;
3365#endif
3366 }
3367#else /* R/O configuration */
3368 if (res == FR_OK) {
3369 if (dj.fn[NSFLAG11] & NS_NONAME0x80) { /* Origin directory itself? */
3370 res = FR_INVALID_NAME;
3371 } else {
3372 if (dj.obj.attr & AM_DIR0x10) { /* It is a directory */
3373 res = FR_NO_FILE;
3374 }
3375 }
3376 }
3377#endif
3378
3379 if (res == FR_OK) {
3380#if _FS_EXFAT1
3381 if (fs->fs_type == FS_EXFAT4) {
3382 fp->obj.sclust = ld_dword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FstClus52); /* Get allocation info */
3383 fp->obj.objsize = ld_qword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FileSize56);
3384 fp->obj.stat = fs->dirbuf[XDIR_GenFlags33] & 2;
3385 fp->obj.c_scl = dj.obj.sclust;
3386 fp->obj.c_size = ((DWORD)dj.obj.objsize & 0xFFFFFF00) | dj.obj.stat;
3387 fp->obj.c_ofs = dj.blk_ofs;
3388 } else
3389#endif
3390 {
3391 fp->obj.sclust = ld_clust(fs, dj.dir); /* Get allocation info */
3392 fp->obj.objsize = ld_dword(dj.dir + DIR_FileSize28);
3393 }
3394#if _USE_FASTSEEK0
3395 fp->cltbl = 0; /* Disable fast seek mode */
3396#endif
3397 fp->obj.fs = fs; /* Validate the file object */
3398 fp->obj.id = fs->id;
3399 fp->flag = mode; /* Set file access mode */
3400 fp->err = 0; /* Clear error flag */
3401 fp->sect = 0; /* Invalidate current data sector */
3402 fp->fptr = 0; /* Set file pointer top of the file */
3403#if !_FS_READONLY0
3404#if !_FS_TINY0
3405 mem_set(fp->buf, 0, _MAX_SS512); /* Clear sector buffer */
3406#endif
3407 if ((mode & FA_SEEKEND0x20) && fp->obj.objsize > 0) { /* Seek to end of file if FA_OPEN_APPEND is specified */
3408 fp->fptr = fp->obj.objsize; /* Offset to seek */
3409 bcs = (DWORD)fs->csize * SS(fs)((UINT)512); /* Cluster size in byte */
3410 clst = fp->obj.sclust; /* Follow the cluster chain */
3411 for (ofs = fp->obj.objsize; res == FR_OK && ofs > bcs; ofs -= bcs) {
3412 clst = get_fat(&fp->obj, clst);
3413 if (clst <= 1) res = FR_INT_ERR;
3414 if (clst == 0xFFFFFFFF) res = FR_DISK_ERR;
3415 }
3416 fp->clust = clst;
3417 if (res == FR_OK && ofs % SS(fs)((UINT)512)) { /* Fill sector buffer if not on the sector boundary */
3418 if ((sc = clust2sect(fs, clst)) == 0) {
3419 res = FR_INT_ERR;
3420 } else {
3421 fp->sect = sc + (DWORD)(ofs / SS(fs)((UINT)512));
3422#if !_FS_TINY0
3423 if (disk_read(fs->drv, fp->buf, fp->sect, 1) != RES_OK) res = FR_DISK_ERR;
3424#endif
3425 }
3426 }
3427 }
3428#endif
3429 }
3430
3431 FREE_NAMBUF()ff_memfree(lfn);
3432 }
3433
3434 if (res != FR_OK) fp->obj.fs = 0; /* Invalidate file object on error */
3435
3436 LEAVE_FF(fs, res)return res;
3437}
3438
3439
3440
3441
3442/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3443/* Read File */
3444/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3445
3446FRESULT f_read (
3447 FIL* fp, /* Pointer to the file object */
3448 void* buff, /* Pointer to data buffer */
3449 UINT btr, /* Number of bytes to read */
3450 UINT* br /* Pointer to number of bytes read */
3451)
3452{
3453 FRESULT res;
3454 FATFS *fs;
3455 DWORD clst, sect;
3456 FSIZE_t remain;
3457 UINT rcnt, cc, csect;
3458 BYTE *rbuff = (BYTE*)buff;
3459
3460
3461 *br = 0; /* Clear read byte counter */
3462 res = validate(&fp->obj, &fs); /* Check validity of the file object */
3463 if (res != FR_OK || (res = (FRESULT)fp->err) != FR_OK) LEAVE_FF(fs, res)return res; /* Check validity */
3464 if (!(fp->flag & FA_READ0x01)) LEAVE_FF(fs, FR_DENIED)return FR_DENIED; /* Check access mode */
3465 remain = fp->obj.objsize - fp->fptr;
3466 if (btr > remain) btr = (UINT)remain; /* Truncate btr by remaining bytes */
3467
3468 for ( ; btr; /* Repeat until all data read */
3469 rbuff += rcnt, fp->fptr += rcnt, *br += rcnt, btr -= rcnt) {
3470 if (fp->fptr % SS(fs)((UINT)512) == 0) { /* On the sector boundary? */
3471 csect = (UINT)(fp->fptr / SS(fs)((UINT)512) & (fs->csize - 1)); /* Sector offset in the cluster */
3472 if (csect == 0) { /* On the cluster boundary? */
3473 if (fp->fptr == 0) { /* On the top of the file? */
3474 clst = fp->obj.sclust; /* Follow cluster chain from the origin */
3475 } else { /* Middle or end of the file */
3476#if _USE_FASTSEEK0
3477 if (fp->cltbl) {
3478 clst = clmt_clust(fp, fp->fptr); /* Get cluster# from the CLMT */
3479 } else
3480#endif
3481 {
3482 clst = get_fat(&fp->obj, fp->clust); /* Follow cluster chain on the FAT */
3483 }
3484 }
3485 if (clst < 2) ABORT(fs, FR_INT_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_INT_ERR); return FR_INT_ERR; };
3486 if (clst == 0xFFFFFFFF) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; };
3487 fp->clust = clst; /* Update current cluster */
3488 }
3489 sect = clust2sect(fs, fp->clust); /* Get current sector */
3490 if (!sect) ABORT(fs, FR_INT_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_INT_ERR); return FR_INT_ERR; };
3491 sect += csect;
3492 cc = btr / SS(fs)((UINT)512); /* When remaining bytes >= sector size, */
3493 if (cc) { /* Read maximum contiguous sectors directly */
3494 if (csect + cc > fs->csize) { /* Clip at cluster boundary */
3495 cc = fs->csize - csect;
3496 }
3497 if (disk_read(fs->drv, rbuff, sect, cc) != RES_OK) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; };
3498#if !_FS_READONLY0 && _FS_MINIMIZE0 <= 2 /* Replace one of the read sectors with cached data if it contains a dirty sector */
3499#if _FS_TINY0
3500 if (fs->wflag && fs->winsect - sect < cc) {
3501 mem_cpy(rbuff + ((fs->winsect - sect) * SS(fs)((UINT)512)), fs->win, SS(fs)((UINT)512));
3502 }
3503#else
3504 if ((fp->flag & FA_DIRTY0x80) && fp->sect - sect < cc) {
3505 mem_cpy(rbuff + ((fp->sect - sect) * SS(fs)((UINT)512)), fp->buf, SS(fs)((UINT)512));
3506 }
3507#endif
3508#endif
3509 rcnt = SS(fs)((UINT)512) * cc; /* Number of bytes transferred */
3510 continue;
3511 }
3512#if !_FS_TINY0
3513 if (fp->sect != sect) { /* Load data sector if not in cache */
3514#if !_FS_READONLY0
3515 if (fp->flag & FA_DIRTY0x80) { /* Write-back dirty sector cache */
3516 if (disk_write(fs->drv, fp->buf, fp->sect, 1) != RES_OK) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; };
3517 fp->flag &= (BYTE)~FA_DIRTY0x80;
3518 }
3519#endif
3520 if (disk_read(fs->drv, fp->buf, sect, 1) != RES_OK) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; }; /* Fill sector cache */
3521 }
3522#endif
3523 fp->sect = sect;
3524 }
3525 rcnt = SS(fs)((UINT)512) - (UINT)fp->fptr % SS(fs)((UINT)512); /* Number of bytes left in the sector */
3526 if (rcnt > btr) rcnt = btr; /* Clip it by btr if needed */
3527#if _FS_TINY0
3528 if (move_window(fs, fp->sect) != FR_OK) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; }; /* Move sector window */
3529 mem_cpy(rbuff, fs->win + fp->fptr % SS(fs)((UINT)512), rcnt); /* Extract partial sector */
3530#else
3531 mem_cpy(rbuff, fp->buf + fp->fptr % SS(fs)((UINT)512), rcnt); /* Extract partial sector */
3532#endif
3533 }
3534
3535 LEAVE_FF(fs, FR_OK)return FR_OK;
3536}
3537
3538
3539
3540
3541#if !_FS_READONLY0
3542/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3543/* Write File */
3544/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3545
3546FRESULT f_write (
3547 FIL* fp, /* Pointer to the file object */
3548 const void* buff, /* Pointer to the data to be written */
3549 UINT btw, /* Number of bytes to write */
3550 UINT* bw /* Pointer to number of bytes written */
3551)
3552{
3553 FRESULT res;
3554 FATFS *fs;
3555 DWORD clst, sect;
3556 UINT wcnt, cc, csect;
3557 const BYTE *wbuff = (const BYTE*)buff;
3558
3559
3560 *bw = 0; /* Clear write byte counter */
3561 res = validate(&fp->obj, &fs); /* Check validity of the file object */
3562 if (res != FR_OK || (res = (FRESULT)fp->err) != FR_OK) LEAVE_FF(fs, res)return res; /* Check validity */
3563 if (!(fp->flag & FA_WRITE0x02)) LEAVE_FF(fs, FR_DENIED)return FR_DENIED; /* Check access mode */
3564
3565 /* Check fptr wrap-around (file size cannot reach 4GiB on FATxx) */
3566 if ((!_FS_EXFAT1 || fs->fs_type != FS_EXFAT4) && (DWORD)(fp->fptr + btw) < (DWORD)fp->fptr) {
3567 btw = (UINT)(0xFFFFFFFF - (DWORD)fp->fptr);
3568 }
3569
3570 for ( ; btw; /* Repeat until all data written */
3571 wbuff += wcnt, fp->fptr += wcnt, fp->obj.objsize = (fp->fptr > fp->obj.objsize) ? fp->fptr : fp->obj.objsize, *bw += wcnt, btw -= wcnt) {
3572 if (fp->fptr % SS(fs)((UINT)512) == 0) { /* On the sector boundary? */
3573 csect = (UINT)(fp->fptr / SS(fs)((UINT)512)) & (fs->csize - 1); /* Sector offset in the cluster */
3574 if (csect == 0) { /* On the cluster boundary? */
3575 if (fp->fptr == 0) { /* On the top of the file? */
3576 clst = fp->obj.sclust; /* Follow from the origin */
3577 if (clst == 0) { /* If no cluster is allocated, */
3578 clst = create_chain(&fp->obj, 0); /* create a new cluster chain */
3579 }
3580 } else { /* On the middle or end of the file */
3581#if _USE_FASTSEEK0
3582 if (fp->cltbl) {
3583 clst = clmt_clust(fp, fp->fptr); /* Get cluster# from the CLMT */
3584 } else
3585#endif
3586 {
3587 clst = create_chain(&fp->obj, fp->clust); /* Follow or stretch cluster chain on the FAT */
3588 }
3589 }
3590 if (clst == 0) break; /* Could not allocate a new cluster (disk full) */
3591 if (clst == 1) ABORT(fs, FR_INT_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_INT_ERR); return FR_INT_ERR; };
3592 if (clst == 0xFFFFFFFF) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; };
3593 fp->clust = clst; /* Update current cluster */
3594 if (fp->obj.sclust == 0) fp->obj.sclust = clst; /* Set start cluster if the first write */
3595 }
3596#if _FS_TINY0
3597 if (fs->winsect == fp->sect && sync_window(fs) != FR_OK) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; }; /* Write-back sector cache */
3598#else
3599 if (fp->flag & FA_DIRTY0x80) { /* Write-back sector cache */
3600 if (disk_write(fs->drv, fp->buf, fp->sect, 1) != RES_OK) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; };
3601 fp->flag &= (BYTE)~FA_DIRTY0x80;
3602 }
3603#endif
3604 sect = clust2sect(fs, fp->clust); /* Get current sector */
3605 if (!sect) ABORT(fs, FR_INT_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_INT_ERR); return FR_INT_ERR; };
3606 sect += csect;
3607 cc = btw / SS(fs)((UINT)512); /* When remaining bytes >= sector size, */
3608 if (cc) { /* Write maximum contiguous sectors directly */
3609 if (csect + cc > fs->csize) { /* Clip at cluster boundary */
3610 cc = fs->csize - csect;
3611 }
3612 if (disk_write(fs->drv, wbuff, sect, cc) != RES_OK) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; };
3613#if _FS_MINIMIZE0 <= 2
3614#if _FS_TINY0
3615 if (fs->winsect - sect < cc) { /* Refill sector cache if it gets invalidated by the direct write */
3616 mem_cpy(fs->win, wbuff + ((fs->winsect - sect) * SS(fs)((UINT)512)), SS(fs)((UINT)512));
3617 fs->wflag = 0;
3618 }
3619#else
3620 if (fp->sect - sect < cc) { /* Refill sector cache if it gets invalidated by the direct write */
3621 mem_cpy(fp->buf, wbuff + ((fp->sect - sect) * SS(fs)((UINT)512)), SS(fs)((UINT)512));
3622 fp->flag &= (BYTE)~FA_DIRTY0x80;
3623 }
3624#endif
3625#endif
3626 wcnt = SS(fs)((UINT)512) * cc; /* Number of bytes transferred */
3627 continue;
3628 }
3629#if _FS_TINY0
3630 if (fp->fptr >= fp->obj.objsize) { /* Avoid silly cache filling on the growing edge */
3631 if (sync_window(fs) != FR_OK) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; };
3632 fs->winsect = sect;
3633 }
3634#else
3635 if (fp->sect != sect && /* Fill sector cache with file data */
3636 fp->fptr < fp->obj.objsize &&
3637 disk_read(fs->drv, fp->buf, sect, 1) != RES_OK) {
3638 ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; };
3639 }
3640#endif
3641 fp->sect = sect;
3642 }
3643 wcnt = SS(fs)((UINT)512) - (UINT)fp->fptr % SS(fs)((UINT)512); /* Number of bytes left in the sector */
3644 if (wcnt > btw) wcnt = btw; /* Clip it by btw if needed */
3645#if _FS_TINY0
3646 if (move_window(fs, fp->sect) != FR_OK) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; }; /* Move sector window */
3647 mem_cpy(fs->win + fp->fptr % SS(fs)((UINT)512), wbuff, wcnt); /* Fit data to the sector */
3648 fs->wflag = 1;
3649#else
3650 mem_cpy(fp->buf + fp->fptr % SS(fs)((UINT)512), wbuff, wcnt); /* Fit data to the sector */
3651 fp->flag |= FA_DIRTY0x80;
3652#endif
3653 }
3654
3655 fp->flag |= FA_MODIFIED0x40; /* Set file change flag */
3656
3657 LEAVE_FF(fs, FR_OK)return FR_OK;
3658}
3659
3660
3661
3662
3663/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3664/* Synchronize the File */
3665/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3666
3667FRESULT f_sync (
3668 FIL* fp /* Pointer to the file object */
3669)
3670{
3671 FRESULT res;
3672 FATFS *fs;
3673 DWORD tm;
3674 BYTE *dir;
3675#if _FS_EXFAT1
3676 DEF_NAMBUFWCHAR *lfn;
3677#endif
3678
3679 res = validate(&fp->obj, &fs); /* Check validity of the file object */
3680 if (res == FR_OK) {
3681 if (fp->flag & FA_MODIFIED0x40) { /* Is there any change to the file? */
3682#if !_FS_TINY0
3683 if (fp->flag & FA_DIRTY0x80) { /* Write-back cached data if needed */
3684 if (disk_write(fs->drv, fp->buf, fp->sect, 1) != RES_OK) LEAVE_FF(fs, FR_DISK_ERR)return FR_DISK_ERR;
3685 fp->flag &= (BYTE)~FA_DIRTY0x80;
3686 }
3687#endif
3688 /* Update the directory entry */
3689 tm = GET_FATTIME()get_fattime(); /* Modified time */
3690#if _FS_EXFAT1
3691 if (fs->fs_type == FS_EXFAT4) {
3692 res = fill_fat_chain(&fp->obj); /* Create FAT chain if needed */
3693 if (res == FR_OK) {
3694 DIR dj;
3695
3696 INIT_NAMBUF(fs){ lfn = ff_memalloc((255 +1)*2 + 32*19); if (!lfn) return FR_NOT_ENOUGH_CORE
; (fs)->lfnbuf = lfn; (fs)->dirbuf = (BYTE*)(lfn+255 +1
); };
3697 res = load_obj_dir(&dj, &fp->obj); /* Load directory entry block */
3698 if (res == FR_OK) {
3699 fs->dirbuf[XDIR_Attr4] |= AM_ARC0x20; /* Set archive bit */
3700 fs->dirbuf[XDIR_GenFlags33] = fp->obj.stat | 1; /* Update file allocation info */
3701 st_dword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FstClus52, fp->obj.sclust);
3702 st_qword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FileSize56, fp->obj.objsize);
3703 st_qword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_ValidFileSize40, fp->obj.objsize);
3704 st_dword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_ModTime12, tm); /* Update modified time */
3705 fs->dirbuf[XDIR_ModTime1021] = 0;
3706 st_dword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_AccTime16, 0);
3707 res = store_xdir(&dj); /* Restore it to the directory */
3708 if (res == FR_OK) {
3709 res = sync_fs(fs);
3710 fp->flag &= (BYTE)~FA_MODIFIED0x40;
3711 }
3712 }
3713 FREE_NAMBUF()ff_memfree(lfn);
3714 }
3715 } else
3716#endif
3717 {
3718 res = move_window(fs, fp->dir_sect);
3719 if (res == FR_OK) {
3720 dir = fp->dir_ptr;
3721 dir[DIR_Attr11] |= AM_ARC0x20; /* Set archive bit */
3722 st_clust(fp->obj.fs, dir, fp->obj.sclust); /* Update file allocation info */
3723 st_dword(dir + DIR_FileSize28, (DWORD)fp->obj.objsize); /* Update file size */
3724 st_dword(dir + DIR_ModTime22, tm); /* Update modified time */
3725 st_word(dir + DIR_LstAccDate18, 0);
3726 fs->wflag = 1;
3727 res = sync_fs(fs); /* Restore it to the directory */
3728 fp->flag &= (BYTE)~FA_MODIFIED0x40;
3729 }
3730 }
3731 }
3732 }
3733
3734 LEAVE_FF(fs, res)return res;
3735}
3736
3737#endif /* !_FS_READONLY */
3738
3739
3740
3741
3742/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3743/* Close File */
3744/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3745
3746FRESULT f_close (
3747 FIL* fp /* Pointer to the file object to be closed */
3748)
3749{
3750 FRESULT res;
3751 FATFS *fs;
3752
3753#if !_FS_READONLY0
3754 res = f_sync(fp); /* Flush cached data */
3755 if (res == FR_OK)
3756#endif
3757 {
3758 res = validate(&fp->obj, &fs); /* Lock volume */
3759 if (res == FR_OK) {
3760#if _FS_LOCK0 != 0
3761 res = dec_lock(fp->obj.lockid); /* Decrement file open counter */
3762 if (res == FR_OK)
3763#endif
3764 {
3765 fp->obj.fs = 0; /* Invalidate file object */
3766 }
3767#if _FS_REENTRANT0
3768 unlock_fs(fs, FR_OK); /* Unlock volume */
3769#endif
3770 }
3771 }
3772 return res;
3773}

3780/* Change Current Directory or Current Drive, Get Current Directory */
3781/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3782
3783#if _VOLUMES1 >= 2
3784FRESULT f_chdrive (
3785 const TCHAR* path /* Drive number */
3786)
3787{

3789
3790
3791 /* Get logical drive number */
3792 vol = get_ldnumber(&path);
3793 if (vol < 0) return FR_INVALID_DRIVE;
3794
3795 CurrVol = (BYTE)vol; /* Set it as current volume */
3796
3797 return FR_OK;
3798}

3800
3801
3802FRESULT f_chdir (
3803 const TCHAR* path /* Pointer to the directory path */
3804)
3805{
3806 FRESULT res;
3807 DIR dj;
3808 FATFS *fs;
3809 DEF_NAMBUFWCHAR *lfn;
3810
3811 /* Get logical drive */
3812 res = find_volume(&path, &fs, 0);
3813 if (res == FR_OK) {
3814 dj.obj.fs = fs;
3815 INIT_NAMBUF(fs){ lfn = ff_memalloc((255 +1)*2 + 32*19); if (!lfn) return FR_NOT_ENOUGH_CORE
; (fs)->lfnbuf = lfn; (fs)->dirbuf = (BYTE*)(lfn+255 +1
); };
3816 res = follow_path(&dj, path); /* Follow the path */
3817 if (res == FR_OK) { /* Follow completed */
3818 if (dj.fn[NSFLAG11] & NS_NONAME0x80) {
3819 fs->cdir = dj.obj.sclust; /* It is the start directory itself */
3820#if _FS_EXFAT1
3821 if (fs->fs_type == FS_EXFAT4) {
3822 fs->cdc_scl = dj.obj.c_scl;
3823 fs->cdc_size = dj.obj.c_size;
3824 fs->cdc_ofs = dj.obj.c_ofs;
3825 }
3826#endif
3827 } else {
3828 if (dj.obj.attr & AM_DIR0x10) { /* It is a sub-directory */
3829#if _FS_EXFAT1
3830 if (fs->fs_type == FS_EXFAT4) {
3831 fs->cdir = ld_dword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FstClus52); /* Sub-directory cluster */
3832 fs->cdc_scl = dj.obj.sclust; /* Save containing directory information */
3833 fs->cdc_size = ((DWORD)dj.obj.objsize & 0xFFFFFF00) | dj.obj.stat;
3834 fs->cdc_ofs = dj.blk_ofs;
3835 } else
3836#endif
3837 {
3838 fs->cdir = ld_clust(fs, dj.dir); /* Sub-directory cluster */
3839 }
3840 } else {
3841 res = FR_NO_PATH; /* Reached but a file */
3842 }
3843 }
3844 }
3845 FREE_NAMBUF()ff_memfree(lfn);
3846 if (res == FR_NO_FILE) res = FR_NO_PATH;
3847 }
3848
3849 LEAVE_FF(fs, res)return res;
3850}
3851
3852
3853#if _FS_RPATH2 >= 2
3854FRESULT f_getcwd (
3855 TCHAR* buff, /* Pointer to the directory path */
3856 UINT len /* Size of path */
3857)
3858{
3859 FRESULT res;
3860 DIR dj;
3861 FATFS *fs;
3862 UINT i, n;
3863 DWORD ccl;
3864 TCHAR *tp;
3865 FILINFO fno;
3866 DEF_NAMBUFWCHAR *lfn;
3867
3868
3869 *buff = 0;
3870 /* Get logical drive */
3871 res = find_volume((const TCHAR**)&buff, &fs, 0); /* Get current volume */
3872 if (res == FR_OK) {
3873 dj.obj.fs = fs;
3874 INIT_NAMBUF(fs){ lfn = ff_memalloc((255 +1)*2 + 32*19); if (!lfn) return FR_NOT_ENOUGH_CORE
; (fs)->lfnbuf = lfn; (fs)->dirbuf = (BYTE*)(lfn+255 +1
); };
3875 i = len; /* Bottom of buffer (directory stack base) */
3876 if (!_FS_EXFAT1 || fs->fs_type != FS_EXFAT4) { /* (Cannot do getcwd on exFAT and returns root path) */
3877 dj.obj.sclust = fs->cdir; /* Start to follow upper directory from current directory */
3878 while ((ccl = dj.obj.sclust) != 0) { /* Repeat while current directory is a sub-directory */
3879 res = dir_sdi(&dj, 1 * SZDIRE32); /* Get parent directory */
3880 if (res != FR_OK) break;
3881 res = move_window(fs, dj.sect);
3882 if (res != FR_OK) break;
3883 dj.obj.sclust = ld_clust(fs, dj.dir); /* Goto parent directory */
3884 res = dir_sdi(&dj, 0);
3885 if (res != FR_OK) break;
3886 do { /* Find the entry links to the child directory */
3887 res = dir_read(&dj, 0);
3888 if (res != FR_OK) break;
3889 if (ccl == ld_clust(fs, dj.dir)) break; /* Found the entry */
3890 res = dir_next(&dj, 0);
3891 } while (res == FR_OK);
3892 if (res == FR_NO_FILE) res = FR_INT_ERR;/* It cannot be 'not found'. */
3893 if (res != FR_OK) break;
3894 get_fileinfo(&dj, &fno); /* Get the directory name and push it to the buffer */
3895 for (n = 0; fno.fname[n]; n++) ;
3896 if (i < n + 3) {
3897 res = FR_NOT_ENOUGH_CORE; break;
3898 }
3899 while (n) buff[--i] = fno.fname[--n];
3900 buff[--i] = '/';
3901 }
3902 }
3903 tp = buff;
3904 if (res == FR_OK) {
3905#if _VOLUMES1 >= 2
3906 *tp++ = '0' + CurrVol; /* Put drive number */
3907 *tp++ = ':';
3908#endif
3909 if (i == len) { /* Root-directory */
3910 *tp++ = '/';
3911 } else { /* Sub-directroy */
3912 do /* Add stacked path str */
3913 *tp++ = buff[i++];
3914 while (i < len);
3915 }
3916 }
3917 *tp = 0;
3918 FREE_NAMBUF()ff_memfree(lfn);
3919 }
3920
3921 LEAVE_FF(fs, res)return res;
3922}
3923
3924#endif /* _FS_RPATH >= 2 */
3925#endif /* _FS_RPATH >= 1 */
3926

3928
3929#if _FS_MINIMIZE0 <= 2
3930/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3931/* Seek File R/W Pointer */
3932/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
3933
3934FRESULT f_lseek (
3935 FIL* fp, /* Pointer to the file object */
3936 FSIZE_t ofs /* File pointer from top of file */
3937)
3938{
3939 FRESULT res;
3940 FATFS *fs;
3941 DWORD clst, bcs, nsect;
3942 FSIZE_t ifptr;
3943#if _USE_FASTSEEK0
3944 DWORD cl, pcl, ncl, tcl, dsc, tlen, ulen, *tbl;
3945#endif
3946
3947 res = validate(&fp->obj, &fs); /* Check validity of the file object */
3948 if (res != FR_OK || (res = (FRESULT)fp->err) != FR_OK) LEAVE_FF(fs, res)return res; /* Check validity */
3949#if _USE_FASTSEEK0
3950 if (fp->cltbl) { /* Fast seek */
3951 if (ofs == CREATE_LINKMAP((FSIZE_t)0 - 1)) { /* Create CLMT */
3952 tbl = fp->cltbl;
3953 tlen = *tbl++; ulen = 2; /* Given table size and required table size */
3954 cl = fp->obj.sclust; /* Origin of the chain */
3955 if (cl) {
3956 do {
3957 /* Get a fragment */
3958 tcl = cl; ncl = 0; ulen += 2; /* Top, length and used items */
3959 do {
3960 pcl = cl; ncl++;
3961 cl = get_fat(&fp->obj, cl);
3962 if (cl <= 1) ABORT(fs, FR_INT_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_INT_ERR); return FR_INT_ERR; };
3963 if (cl == 0xFFFFFFFF) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; };
3964 } while (cl == pcl + 1);
3965 if (ulen <= tlen) { /* Store the length and top of the fragment */
3966 *tbl++ = ncl; *tbl++ = tcl;
3967 }
3968 } while (cl < fs->n_fatent); /* Repeat until end of chain */
3969 }
3970 *fp->cltbl = ulen; /* Number of items used */
3971 if (ulen <= tlen) {
3972 *tbl = 0; /* Terminate table */
3973 } else {
3974 res = FR_NOT_ENOUGH_CORE; /* Given table size is smaller than required */
3975 }
3976 } else { /* Fast seek */
3977 if (ofs > fp->obj.objsize) ofs = fp->obj.objsize; /* Clip offset at the file size */
3978 fp->fptr = ofs; /* Set file pointer */
3979 if (ofs) {
3980 fp->clust = clmt_clust(fp, ofs - 1);
3981 dsc = clust2sect(fs, fp->clust);
3982 if (!dsc) ABORT(fs, FR_INT_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_INT_ERR); return FR_INT_ERR; };
3983 dsc += (DWORD)((ofs - 1) / SS(fs)((UINT)512)) & (fs->csize - 1);
3984 if (fp->fptr % SS(fs)((UINT)512) && dsc != fp->sect) { /* Refill sector cache if needed */
3985#if !_FS_TINY0
3986#if !_FS_READONLY0
3987 if (fp->flag & FA_DIRTY0x80) { /* Write-back dirty sector cache */
3988 if (disk_write(fs->drv, fp->buf, fp->sect, 1) != RES_OK) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; };
3989 fp->flag &= (BYTE)~FA_DIRTY0x80;
3990 }
3991#endif
3992 if (disk_read(fs->drv, fp->buf, dsc, 1) != RES_OK) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; }; /* Load current sector */
3993#endif
3994 fp->sect = dsc;
3995 }
3996 }
3997 }
3998 } else
3999#endif
4000
4001 /* Normal Seek */
4002 {
4003#if _FS_EXFAT1
4004 if (fs->fs_type != FS_EXFAT4 && ofs >= 0x100000000) ofs = 0xFFFFFFFF; /* Clip at 4GiB-1 if at FATxx */
4005#endif
4006 if (ofs > fp->obj.objsize && (_FS_READONLY0 || !(fp->flag & FA_WRITE0x02))) { /* In read-only mode, clip offset with the file size */
4007 ofs = fp->obj.objsize;
4008 }
4009 ifptr = fp->fptr;
4010 fp->fptr = nsect = 0;
4011 if (ofs) {
4012 bcs = (DWORD)fs->csize * SS(fs)((UINT)512); /* Cluster size (byte) */
4013 if (ifptr > 0 &&
4014 (ofs - 1) / bcs >= (ifptr - 1) / bcs) { /* When seek to same or following cluster, */
4015 fp->fptr = (ifptr - 1) & ~(FSIZE_t)(bcs - 1); /* start from the current cluster */
4016 ofs -= fp->fptr;
4017 clst = fp->clust;
4018 } else { /* When seek to back cluster, */
4019 clst = fp->obj.sclust; /* start from the first cluster */
4020#if !_FS_READONLY0
4021 if (clst == 0) { /* If no cluster chain, create a new chain */
4022 clst = create_chain(&fp->obj, 0);
4023 if (clst == 1) ABORT(fs, FR_INT_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_INT_ERR); return FR_INT_ERR; };
4024 if (clst == 0xFFFFFFFF) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; };
4025 fp->obj.sclust = clst;
4026 }
4027#endif
4028 fp->clust = clst;
4029 }
4030 if (clst != 0) {
4031 while (ofs > bcs) { /* Cluster following loop */
4032 ofs -= bcs; fp->fptr += bcs;
4033#if !_FS_READONLY0
4034 if (fp->flag & FA_WRITE0x02) { /* Check if in write mode or not */
4035 if (_FS_EXFAT1 && fp->fptr > fp->obj.objsize) { /* No FAT chain object needs correct objsize to generate FAT value */
4036 fp->obj.objsize = fp->fptr;
4037 fp->flag |= FA_MODIFIED0x40;
4038 }
4039 clst = create_chain(&fp->obj, clst); /* Follow chain with forceed stretch */
4040 if (clst == 0) { /* Clip file size in case of disk full */
4041 ofs = 0; break;
4042 }
4043 } else
4044#endif
4045 {
4046 clst = get_fat(&fp->obj, clst); /* Follow cluster chain if not in write mode */
4047 }
4048 if (clst == 0xFFFFFFFF) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; };
4049 if (clst <= 1 || clst >= fs->n_fatent) ABORT(fs, FR_INT_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_INT_ERR); return FR_INT_ERR; };
4050 fp->clust = clst;
4051 }
4052 fp->fptr += ofs;
4053 if (ofs % SS(fs)((UINT)512)) {
4054 nsect = clust2sect(fs, clst); /* Current sector */
4055 if (!nsect) ABORT(fs, FR_INT_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_INT_ERR); return FR_INT_ERR; };
4056 nsect += (DWORD)(ofs / SS(fs)((UINT)512));
4057 }
4058 }
4059 }
4060 if (!_FS_READONLY0 && fp->fptr > fp->obj.objsize) { /* Set file change flag if the file size is extended */
4061 fp->obj.objsize = fp->fptr;
4062 fp->flag |= FA_MODIFIED0x40;
4063 }
4064 if (fp->fptr % SS(fs)((UINT)512) && nsect != fp->sect) { /* Fill sector cache if needed */
4065#if !_FS_TINY0
4066#if !_FS_READONLY0
4067 if (fp->flag & FA_DIRTY0x80) { /* Write-back dirty sector cache */
4068 if (disk_write(fs->drv, fp->buf, fp->sect, 1) != RES_OK) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; };
4069 fp->flag &= (BYTE)~FA_DIRTY0x80;
4070 }
4071#endif
4072 if (disk_read(fs->drv, fp->buf, nsect, 1) != RES_OK) ABORT(fs, FR_DISK_ERR){ fp->err = (BYTE)(FR_DISK_ERR); return FR_DISK_ERR; }; /* Fill sector cache */
4073#endif
4074 fp->sect = nsect;
4075 }
4076 }
4077
4078 LEAVE_FF(fs, res)return res;
4079}
4080
4081
4082
4083#if _FS_MINIMIZE0 <= 1
4084/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
4085/* Create a Directory Object */
4086/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
4087
4088FRESULT f_opendir (
4089 DIR* dp, /* Pointer to directory object to create */
4090 const TCHAR* path /* Pointer to the directory path */
4091)
4092{
4093 FRESULT res;
4094 FATFS *fs;
4095 _FDID *obj;
4096 DEF_NAMBUFWCHAR *lfn;
4097
4098
4099 if (!dp) return FR_INVALID_OBJECT;
4100
4101 /* Get logical drive */
4102 obj = &dp->obj;
4103 res = find_volume(&path, &fs, 0);
4104 if (res == FR_OK) {
4105 obj->fs = fs;
4106 INIT_NAMBUF(fs){ lfn = ff_memalloc((255 +1)*2 + 32*19); if (!lfn) return FR_NOT_ENOUGH_CORE
; (fs)->lfnbuf = lfn; (fs)->dirbuf = (BYTE*)(lfn+255 +1
); };
4107 res = follow_path(dp, path); /* Follow the path to the directory */
4108 if (res == FR_OK) { /* Follow completed */
4109 if (!(dp->fn[NSFLAG11] & NS_NONAME0x80)) { /* It is not the origin directory itself */
4110 if (obj->attr & AM_DIR0x10) { /* This object is a sub-directory */
4111#if _FS_EXFAT1
4112 if (fs->fs_type == FS_EXFAT4) {
4113 obj->c_scl = obj->sclust; /* Save containing directory inforamation */
4114 obj->c_size = ((DWORD)obj->objsize & 0xFFFFFF00) | obj->stat;
4115 obj->c_ofs = dp->blk_ofs;
4116 obj->sclust = ld_dword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FstClus52); /* Get object location and status */
4117 obj->objsize = ld_qword(fs->dirbuf + XDIR_FileSize56);
4118 obj->stat = fs->dirbuf[XDIR_GenFlags33] & 2;
4119 } else
4120#endif
4121 {
4122 obj->sclust = ld_clust(fs, dp->dir); /* Get object location */
4123 }
4124 } else { /* This object is a file */
4125 res = FR_NO_PATH;
4126 }
4127 }
4128 if (res == FR_OK) {
4129 obj->id = fs->id;
4130 res = dir_sdi(dp, 0); /* Rewind directory */
4131#if _FS_LOCK0 != 0
4132 if (res == FR_OK) {
4133 if (obj->sclust) {
4134 obj->lockid = inc_lock(dp, 0); /* Lock the sub directory */
4135 if (!obj->lockid) res = FR_TOO_MANY_OPEN_FILES;
4136 } else {
4137 obj->lockid = 0; /* Root directory need not to be locked */
4138 }
4139 }
4140#endif
4141 }
4142 }
4143 FREE_NAMBUF()ff_memfree(lfn);
4144 if (res == FR_NO_FILE) res = FR_NO_PATH;
4145 }
4146 if (res != FR_OK) obj->fs = 0; /* Invalidate the directory object if function faild */
4147
4148 LEAVE_FF(fs, res)return res;
4149}

4154/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
4155/* Close Directory */
4156/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
4157
4158FRESULT f_closedir (
4159 DIR *dp /* Pointer to the directory object to be closed */
4160)
4161{
4162 FRESULT res;
4163 FATFS *fs;
4164
4165
4166 res = validate(&dp->obj, &fs); /* Check validity of the file object */
4167 if (res == FR_OK) {
4168#if _FS_LOCK0 != 0
4169 if (dp->obj.lockid) { /* Decrement sub-directory open counter */
4170 res = dec_lock(dp->obj.lockid);
4171 }
4172 if (res == FR_OK)
4173#endif
4174 {
4175 dp->obj.fs = 0; /* Invalidate directory object */
4176 }
4177#if _FS_REENTRANT0
4178 unlock_fs(fs, FR_OK); /* Unlock volume */
4179#endif
4180 }
4181 return res;
4182}

4184
4185
4186
4187/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
4188/* Read Directory Entries in Sequence */
4189/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
4190
4191FRESULT f_readdir (
4192 DIR* dp, /* Pointer to the open directory object */
4193 FILINFO* fno /* Pointer to file information to return */
4194)
4195{
4196 FRESULT res;
4197 FATFS *fs;
4198 DEF_NAMBUFWCHAR *lfn;
4199
4200
4201 res = validate(&dp->obj, &fs); /* Check validity of the directory object */
4202 if (res == FR_OK) {
4203 if (!fno) {
4204 res = dir_sdi(dp, 0); /* Rewind the directory object */
4205 } else {
4206 INIT_NAMBUF(fs){ lfn = ff_memalloc((255 +1)*2 + 32*19); if (!lfn) return FR_NOT_ENOUGH_CORE
; (fs)->lfnbuf = lfn; (fs)->dirbuf = (BYTE*)(lfn+255 +1
); };
4207 res = dir_read(dp, 0); /* Read an item */
4208 if (res == FR_NO_FILE) res = FR_OK; /* Ignore end of directory */
4209 if (res == FR_OK) { /* A valid entry is found */
4210 get_fileinfo(dp, fno); /* Get the object information */
4211 res = dir_next(dp, 0); /* Increment index for next */
4212 if (res == FR_NO_FILE) res = FR_OK; /* Ignore end of directory now */
4213 }
4214 FREE_NAMBUF()ff_memfree(lfn);
4215 }
4216 }
4217 LEAVE_FF(fs, res)return res;
4218}
4219
4220
4221
4222#if _USE_FIND1
4223/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
4224/* Find Next File */
4225/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
4226
4227FRESULT f_findnext (
4228 DIR* dp, /* Pointer to the open directory object */
4229 FILINFO* fno /* Pointer to the file information structure */
4230)
4231{
4232 FRESULT res;
4233
4234
4235 for (;;) {
4236 res = f_readdir(dp, fno); /* Get a directory item */
4237 if (res != FR_OK || !fno || !fno->fname[0]) break; /* Terminate if any error or end of directory */
4238 if (pattern_matching(dp->pat, fno->fname, 0, 0)) break; /* Test for the file name */
4239#if _USE_LFN3 != 0 && _USE_FIND1 == 2
4240 if (pattern_matching(dp->pat, fno->altname, 0, 0)) break; /* Test for alternative name if exist */
4241#endif
4242 }
4243 return res;
4244}

4250/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
4251
4252FRESULT f_findfirst (
4253 DIR* dp, /* Pointer to the blank directory object */
4254 FILINFO* fno, /* Pointer to the file information structure */
4255 const TCHAR* path, /* Pointer to the directory to open */
4256 const TCHAR* pattern /* Pointer to the matching pattern */
4257)
4258{
4259 FRESULT res;
4260
4261
4262 dp->pat = pattern; /* Save pointer to pattern string */
4263 res = f_opendir(dp, path); /* Open the target directory */
4264 if (res == FR_OK) {
4265 res = f_findnext(dp, fno); /* Find the first item */
4266 }
4267 return res;
4268}

4274#if _FS_MINIMIZE0 == 0
4275/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
4276/* Get File Status */
4277/*-----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
4278
4279FRESULT f_stat (
4280 const TCHAR* path, /* Pointer to the file path */
4281 FILINFO* fno /* Pointer to file information to return */
4282)
4283{
4284 FRESULT res;
4285 DIR dj;
4286 DEF_NAMBUFWCHAR *lfn;
4287
4288
4289 /* Get logical drive */
4290 res = find_volume(&path, &dj.obj.fs, 0);
4291 if (res == FR_OK) {
4292 INIT_NAMBUF(dj.obj.fs){ lfn = ff_memalloc((255 +1)*2 + 32*19); if (!lfn) return FR_NOT_ENOUGH_CORE
; (dj.obj.fs)->lfnbuf = lfn; (dj.obj.fs)->dirbuf = (BYTE
*)(lfn+255 +1); };
4293 res = follow_path(&dj, path); /* Follow the file path */
4294 if (res == FR_OK) { /* Follow completed */
4295 if (dj.fn[NSFLAG11] & NS_NONAME0x80) { /* It is origin directory */
4296 res = FR_INVALID_NAME;
4297 } else { /* Found an object */
4298 if (fno) get_fileinfo(&dj, fno);
4299 }
4300 }
4301 FREE_NAMBUF()ff_memfree(lfn);
4302 }
4303
4304 LEAVE_FF(dj.obj.fs, res)return res;
4305}
